< Review>
I've been to a lot of resale shops in my day (quite a few Crossroads in fact) and I've NEVER walked away with a bigger haul than this place. Clearly the Haight is where the most fashionable people sell their clothes. I was definitely in the market for casual clothes and got a variety of t-shirts and sweatshirts, all of which I have been rotating constantly since I visited. Both check-out and dressing room clerks were super sweet. I am actually planning my next visit, even though it's a BART + a Muni ride to get there. It is THAT worth it.< /Review>

< user_id>
103436111892970840349<//user_id>
<Review>Great staff and great selection, if just a hair overpriced. You're bound to find something good.</Review><gmapID>0x8085875330eed5b9:0xa171d97f6dea8821</gmapID></record>
</dataset><record>
<Gmap_id>0x8085875330eed5b9:0xa171d97f6dea8821</Gmap_id>< text>
Tired of hipsters eyeing that prime pickup at H&M on the clearance rack? Mayhaps you want to dress like a hipster. You have your reasons, I won't ask or assume (fun fact: some dress like hipsters so they can get at that cute hipster girl/guy/not sure if that's a girl or a guy *head scratch*) But if you wanna do it on the cheap OR you wanna put together some nice fits for very affordable prices, Crossroads is just your place.

This place is kinda sorta like a thrift shop, but kinda sorta not. You've definitely got your used threads here, to be sure, but a lot of this is top-notch stuff. For example, I spotted an extremely nice coat here for $29. A prime pickup indeed. One might think it to be a bit steep, but check this out b: later that night I saw the same coat at *drumroll* H&M for $69! What the, I can't even... anyhow, there's tons and tons of deals like that to be had here. Again, the threads, like a thrift shop, are often used. But unlike a thrift store pickup, most of what you'll find here is only lightly used. I find a lot of items are just like new. In fact, I would not doubt that a lot of the clothes here ARE new. Ya know, someone needing some gas money. And what's the easiest way to do that? Hmm, how about sacrificing that new skirt or shirt? Boom, petrol in thee ol tank. You get idea.

Probably one of the only downsides, like a thrift shop, is that you won't always find what you like in your size. For instance, they had more of one awesome jacket that I really liked. Albeit, it was only available in S, L, and XL. For me being an M, that meant either looking like a jerky guy trying to show off his muscles in a small jacket OR lookin all baggy like I just stepped outta the 90s and i'm heading to a Droppin' Harmony concert... uh.... Google it. Anyways, that sort of thing will happen from time to time, but it's not the world's largest hassle.

This place is pretty darned great. Great threads on the major cheapo side. If you're stylish, a hipster, a stylish hipster, or you just really wanna get at a hipster like mad crazy yo, you'll definitely wanna hit up Crossroads.< /text>
